<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.4.3 &#20057;&#26041;&#24212;&#19982;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&nbsp;(&#22312;&#36866;&#29992;&#30340;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;)&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#25353;&#29031;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21450;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#36890;&#30693;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#20026;&#27599;&#27425;&#36716;&#35753;&#31614;&#35746;&#32929;&#26435;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall execute a share
transfer contract with respect to each transfer with Party A and/or each Designee (whichever is applicable), in accordance with the provisions
of this Agreement and the Equity Interest Purchase Option Notice regarding the Optioned Interests;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.4.4&nbsp;&#26377;&#20851;&#26041;&#24212;&#31614;&#32626;&#25152;&#26377;&#20854;&#20182;&#25152;&#38656;&#21512;&#21516;&#12289;&#21327;&#35758;&#25110;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#21462;&#24471;&#20840;&#37096;&#25152;&#38656;&#30340;&#25919;&#24220;&#25209;&#20934;&#21644;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#24182;&#37319;&#21462;&#25152;&#26377;&#25152;&#38656;&#34892;&#21160;&#65292;&#22312;&#19981;&#38468;&#24102;&#20219;&#20309;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#30340;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;&#65292;&#23558;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#26377;&#25928;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#36716;&#31227;&#32473;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#24182;&#20351;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#25104;&#20026;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#30331;&#35760;&#22312;&#20876;&#25152;&#26377;&#20154;&#12290;&#20026;&#26412;&#27454;&#21450;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#30446;&#30340;&#65292;&ldquo;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&rdquo;&#21253;&#25324;&#25285;&#20445;&#12289;&#25269;&#25276;&#12289;&#31532;&#19977;&#26041;&#26435;&#21033;&#25110;&#26435;&#30410;&#65292;&#20219;&#20309;&#36141;&#32929;&#26435;&#12289;&#25910;&#36141;&#26435;&#12289;&#20248;&#20808;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#12289;&#25269;&#38144;&#26435;&#12289;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#25187;&#30041;&#25110;&#20854;&#20182;&#25285;&#20445;&#23433;&#25490;&#31561;&#65307;&#20294;&#20026;&#20102;&#26126;&#30830;&#36215;&#35265;&#65292;&#19981;&#21253;&#25324;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#12289;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#12290;&#26412;&#27454;&#21450;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25152;&#35268;&#23450;&#30340;&ldquo;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&rdquo;&#25351;&#30002;&#26041;&#12289;&#20057;&#26041;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#20110;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#31614;&#32626;&#20043;&#26085;&#31614;&#35746;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#65288;&#19979;&#31216;&ldquo;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&rdquo;&#65289;&#65292;&#26681;&#25454;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#65292;&#20057;&#26041;&#20026;&#25285;&#20445;&#19993;&#26041;&#33021;&#23653;&#34892;&#19993;&#26041;&#19982;&#30002;&#26041;&#31614;&#35746;&#30340;&#25511;&#21046;&#21327;&#35758;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20041;&#21153;&#65292;&#32780;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#36136;&#25276;&#20854;&#22312;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#20840;&#37096;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">The relevant Parties shall
execute all other necessary contracts, agreements or documents, obtain all necessary government licenses and permits and take all necessary
actions to transfer valid ownership of the Optioned Interests to Party A and/or the Designee(s), unencumbered by any security interests,
and cause Party A and/or the Designee(s) to become the registered owner(s) of the Optioned Interests. For the purpose of this Section
and this Agreement, &ldquo;security interests&rdquo; shall include securities, mortgages, third party&rsquo;s rights or interests, any stock options,
acquisition right, right of first refusal, right to offset, ownership retention or other security arrangements, but shall be deemed to
exclude any security interest created by this Agreement and Party B&rsquo;s Equity Pledge Agreement. &ldquo;Party B&rsquo;s Equity Pledge Agreement&rdquo;
as used in this Section and this Agreement shall refer to the Equity Pledge Agreement (&ldquo;Party B&rsquo;s Equity Pledge Agreement&rdquo;)
executed by and among Party A, Party B and Party C as of the date hereof, whereby Party B pledges all of its equity interests in Party
C to Party A, in order to guarantee Party C&rsquo;s performance of its obligations under the Control Agreements executed by and between Party
C and Party A.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>2. &#25215;&#35834;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in"><B>Covenants</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1 &#26377;&#20851;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#25215;&#35834;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Covenants regarding Party
C</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#20057;&#26041;&#65288;&#20316;&#20026;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#32929;&#19996;&#65289;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#22312;&#27492;&#25215;&#35834;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 19.05pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 30.6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B (as the shareholders
of Party C) and Party C hereby covenant as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.65pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.65pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 4; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->4<!-- Field: /Sequence -->&nbsp;</P><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.65pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.1 &#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#20197;&#20219;&#20309;&#24418;&#24335;&#34917;&#20805;&#12289;&#26356;&#25913;&#25110;&#20462;&#25913;&#19993;&#26041;&#20844;&#21496;&#31456;&#31243;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#22686;&#21152;&#25110;&#20943;&#23569;&#20854;&#27880;&#20876;&#36164;&#26412;&#65292;&#25110;&#20197;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#24335;&#25913;&#21464;&#20854;&#27880;&#20876;&#36164;&#26412;&#32467;&#26500;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not in any manner supplement, change or amend the articles of association and bylaws of Party C, increase
or decrease its registered capital, or change its structure of registered capital in other manners;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.2 &#25353;&#29031;&#33391;&#22909;&#30340;&#36130;&#21153;&#21644;&#21830;&#19994;&#26631;&#20934;&#21450;&#24815;&#20363;&#65292;&#20445;&#25345;&#20854;&#20844;&#21496;&#30340;&#23384;&#32493;&#65292;&#23457;&#24910;&#22320;&#21450;&#26377;&#25928;&#22320;&#32463;&#33829;&#20854;&#19994;&#21153;&#21644;&#22788;&#29702;&#20107;&#21153;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">They shall maintain Party
C&rsquo;s corporate existence in accordance with good financial and business standards and practices by prudently and effectively operating
its business and handling its affairs;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.3&nbsp;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#31614;&#32626;&#20043;&#26085;&#36215;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#26102;&#38388;&#20986;&#21806;&#12289;&#36716;&#35753;&#12289;&#25269;&#25276;&#25110;&#20197;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#24335;&#22788;&#32622;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#36164;&#20135;&#12289;&#19994;&#21153;&#25110;&#25910;&#20837;&#30340;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#21463;&#30410;&#26435;&#30410;&#65292;&#25110;&#20801;&#35768;&#22312;&#20854;&#19978;&#35774;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#20854;&#20182;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not at any time following the date hereof, sell, transfer, mortgage or dispose of in any manner any assets
of Party C or legal or beneficial interest in the business or revenues of Party C, or allow the encumbrance thereon of any security interest;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.4&nbsp;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#21457;&#29983;&#12289;&#32487;&#25215;&#12289;&#20445;&#35777;&#25110;&#23481;&#35768;&#23384;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#20538;&#21153;&#65292;&#20294;(i)&#27491;&#24120;&#25110;&#26085;&#24120;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#20135;&#29983;&#32780;&#19981;&#26159;&#36890;&#36807;&#20511;&#27454;&#26041;&#24335;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#20538;&#21153;&#65307;&#21644;(ii)&#24050;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#25259;&#38706;&#21644;&#24471;&#21040;&#30002;&#26041;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#30340;&#20538;&#21153;&#38500;&#22806;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not incur, inherit, guarantee or suffer the existence of any debt, except for (i) debts incurred in the
ordinary course of business other than through loans; and (ii) debts disclosed to Party A for which Party A&rsquo;s written consent has been
obtained;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.5 &#19968;&#30452;&#22312;&#27491;&#24120;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#32463;&#33829;&#25152;&#26377;&#19994;&#21153;&#65292;&#20197;&#20445;&#25345;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#36164;&#20135;&#20215;&#20540;&#65292;&#19981;&#36827;&#34892;&#20219;&#20309;&#36275;&#20197;&#24433;&#21709;&#20854;&#32463;&#33829;&#29366;&#20917;&#21644;&#36164;&#20135;&#20215;&#20540;&#30340;&#20316;&#20026;/&#19981;&#20316;&#20026;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">They shall always operate
all of Party C&rsquo;s businesses during the ordinary course of business to maintain the asset value of Party C and refrain from any action/omission
that may affect Party C&rsquo;s operating status and asset value;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.6&nbsp;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#35753;&#19993;&#26041;&#31614;&#35746;&#20219;&#20309;&#37325;&#22823;&#21512;&#21516;&#65292;&#20294;&#22312;&#27491;&#24120;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#31614;&#35746;&#30340;&#21512;&#21516;&#38500;&#22806;(&#23601;&#26412;&#27573;&#32780;&#35328;&#65292;&#22914;&#26524;&#19968;&#20221;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#24635;&#37329;&#39069;&#36229;&#36807;&#20154;&#27665;&#24065;100,000&#20803;&#65292;&#21363;&#34987;&#35270;&#20026;&#37325;&#22823;&#21512;&#21516;)&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not cause Party C to execute any major contract, except the contracts in the ordinary course of business
(for purpose of this subsection, a contract with a price exceeding RMB 100,000 shall be deemed a major contract);</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.7 &#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#19981;&#24471;&#21521;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#25552;&#20379;&#36151;&#27454;&#25110;&#20449;&#36151;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not cause Party C to provide any person with any loan or credit;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.8 &#24212;&#30002;&#26041;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#21521;&#20854;&#25552;&#20379;&#25152;&#26377;&#20851;&#20110;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33829;&#36816;&#21644;&#36130;&#21153;&#29366;&#20917;&#30340;&#36164;&#26009;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">They shall provide Party
A with information on Party C&rsquo;s business operations and financial condition at Party A&rsquo;s request;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.9 &#22914;&#30002;&#26041;&#25552;&#20986;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#24212;&#20174;&#30002;&#26041;&#25509;&#21463;&#30340;&#20445;&#38505;&#20844;&#21496;&#22788;&#36141;&#20080;&#21644;&#25345;&#26377;&#26377;&#20851;&#20854;&#36164;&#20135;&#21644;&#19994;&#21153;&#30340;&#20445;&#38505;&#65292;&#35813;&#20445;&#38505;&#30340;&#37329;&#39069;&#21644;&#38505;&#31181;&#24212;&#19982;&#32463;&#33829;&#31867;&#20284;&#19994;&#21153;&#30340;&#20844;&#21496;&#19968;&#33268;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">If requested by Party A,
they shall procure and maintain insurance in respect of Party C&rsquo;s assets and business from an insurance carrier acceptable to Party A,
at an amount and type of coverage typical for companies that operate similar businesses;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.10 &#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#19981;&#24471;&#19982;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#21512;&#24182;&#25110;&#32852;&#21512;&#65292;&#25110;&#23545;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#36827;&#34892;&#25910;&#36141;&#25110;&#25237;&#36164;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not cause or permit Party C to merge, consolidate with, acquire or invest in any person;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.11 &#23558;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#25110;&#21487;&#33021;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#19982;&#19993;&#26041;&#36164;&#20135;&#12289;&#19994;&#21153;&#25110;&#25910;&#20837;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#35785;&#35772;&#12289;&#20210;&#35009;&#25110;&#34892;&#25919;&#31243;&#24207;&#31435;&#21363;&#36890;&#30693;&#30002;&#26041;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.15pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">They shall immediately notify
Party A of the occurrence or possible occurrence of any litigation, arbitration or administrative proceedings relating to Party C&rsquo;s assets,
business or revenue;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.12&nbsp;&#20026;&#20445;&#25345;&#19993;&#26041;&#23545;&#20854;&#20840;&#37096;&#36164;&#20135;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#65292;&#31614;&#32626;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#37319;&#21462;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#34892;&#21160;&#21644;&#25552;&#20986;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25511;&#21578;&#25110;&#23545;&#25152;&#26377;&#32034;&#20607;&#36827;&#34892;&#24517;&#35201;&#21644;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25239;&#36777;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">To maintain the ownership
by Party C of all of its assets, they shall execute all necessary or appropriate documents, take all necessary or appropriate actions
and file all necessary or appropriate complaints or raise necessary and appropriate defenses against all claims;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.13 &#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#20197;&#20219;&#20309;&#24418;&#24335;&#27966;&#21457;&#32929;&#24687;&#20104;&#21508;&#32929;&#19996;&#65292;&#20294;&#19968;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#24212;&#31435;&#21363;&#23558;&#20854;&#25152;&#26377;&#21487;&#20998;&#37197;&#21033;&#28070;&#20840;&#37096;&#31435;&#21363;&#20998;&#37197;&#32473;&#20854;&#21508;&#32929;&#19996;&#65307;&#21450;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall ensure that Party C shall not in any manner distribute dividends to its shareholders, provided that upon
Party A&rsquo;s written request, Party C shall immediately distribute all distributable profits to its shareholders; and</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1.14 &#26681;&#25454;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#22996;&#20219;&#30001;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#22763;&#20986;&#20219;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33891;&#20107;&#65307;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#26356;&#25442;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33891;&#20107;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">At the request of Party A,
they shall appoint any persons designated by Party A as directors of Party C; without the prior written consent of Party A, they shall
not replace the directors of Party C.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2 &#20057;&#26041;&#30340;&#25215;&#35834;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Covenants of Party B</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#20057;&#26041;&#25215;&#35834;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.7in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B hereby covenants
as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.7in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.1&nbsp;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#20986;&#21806;&#12289;&#36716;&#35753;&#12289;&#25269;&#25276;&#25110;&#20197;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#24335;&#22788;&#32622;&#20854;&#25317;&#26377;&#30340;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#21463;&#30410;&#26435;&#30410;&#65292;&#25110;&#20801;&#35768;&#22312;&#20854;&#19978;&#35774;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#20854;&#20182;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#65292;&#20294;&#26681;&#25454;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#22312;&#35813;&#32929;&#26435;&#19978;&#35774;&#32622;&#30340;&#36136;&#25276;&#21017;&#38500;&#22806;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, Party B shall not sell, transfer, mortgage or dispose of in any other manner any legal or beneficial interest in the
equity interests in Party C held by Party B, or allow the encumbrance thereon of any security interest, except for the pledge placed on
these equity interests in accordance with Party B&rsquo;s Equity Pledge Agreement;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.2&nbsp;&#20419;&#20351;&#19993;&#26041;&#32929;&#19996;&#20250;&#21644;/&#25110;&#33891;&#20107;&#20250;&#19981;&#25209;&#20934;&#22312;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#30340;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;&#65292;&#20986;&#21806;&#12289;&#36716;&#35753;&#12289;&#25269;&#25276;&#25110;&#20197;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#24335;&#22788;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#20057;&#26041;&#25345;&#26377;&#20043;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#21512;&#27861;&#26435;&#30410;&#25110;&#21463;&#30410;&#26435;&#65292;&#25110;&#20801;&#35768;&#22312;&#20854;&#19978;&#35774;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#20854;&#20182;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#65292;&#20294;&#25209;&#20934;&#26681;&#25454;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#22312;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#19978;&#35774;&#32622;&#30340;&#36136;&#25276;&#21017;&#38500;&#22806;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall cause the shareholders&rsquo;
meeting and/or the board of directors of Party C not to approve the sale, transfer, mortgage or disposition in any other manner of any
legal or beneficial interest in the equity interests in Party C held by Party B, or allow the encumbrance thereon of any security interest,
without the prior written consent of Party A, except for the pledge placed on these equity interests in accordance with Party B&rsquo;s Equity
Pledge Agreement;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.3 &#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#30340;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;&#65292;&#23545;&#20110;&#19993;&#26041;&#19982;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#21512;&#24182;&#25110;&#32852;&#21512;&#65292;&#25110;&#23545;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#36827;&#34892;&#25910;&#36141;&#25110;&#25237;&#36164;&#65292;&#20057;&#26041;&#23558;&#20419;&#25104;&#19993;&#26041;&#32929;&#19996;&#20250;&#25110;&#33891;&#20107;&#20250;&#19981;&#20104;&#25209;&#20934;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall cause the shareholders&rsquo;
meeting or the board of directors of Party C not to approve the merger or consolidation with any person, or the acquisition of or investment
in any person, without the prior written consent of Party A;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.4 &#23558;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#25110;&#21487;&#33021;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20851;&#20110;&#20854;&#25152;&#25317;&#26377;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#35785;&#35772;&#12289;&#20210;&#35009;&#25110;&#34892;&#25919;&#31243;&#24207;&#31435;&#21363;&#36890;&#30693;&#30002;&#26041;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall immediately
notify Party A of the occurrence or possible occurrence of any litigation, arbitration or administrative proceedings relating to the equity
interests in Party C held by Party B;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->7<!-- Field: /Sequence -->&nbsp;</P><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.5 &#20419;&#20351;&#19993;&#26041;&#32929;&#19996;&#20250;&#25110;&#33891;&#20107;&#20250;&#34920;&#20915;&#36190;&#25104;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#35268;&#23450;&#30340;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#36716;&#35753;&#24182;&#24212;&#30002;&#26041;&#20043;&#35201;&#27714;&#37319;&#21462;&#20854;&#20182;&#20219;&#20309;&#34892;&#21160;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall cause the shareholders&rsquo;
meeting or the board of directors of Party C to vote their approval of the transfer of the Optioned Interests as set forth in this Agreement
and to take any and all other actions that may be requested by Party A;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.6&nbsp;&#20026;&#20445;&#25345;&#20854;&#23545;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#65292;&#31614;&#32626;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#37319;&#21462;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#34892;&#21160;&#21644;&#25552;&#20986;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25511;&#21578;&#25110;&#23545;&#25152;&#26377;&#32034;&#20607;&#36827;&#34892;&#24517;&#35201;&#21644;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25239;&#36777;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">To the extent necessary to
maintain Party B&rsquo;s ownership in Party C, Party B shall execute all necessary or appropriate documents, take all necessary or appropriate
actions and file all necessary or appropriate complaints or raise necessary and appropriate defenses against all claims;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.7 &#24212;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#22996;&#20219;&#30001;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#22763;&#20986;&#20219;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33891;&#20107;&#21644;/&#25110;&#25191;&#34892;&#33891;&#20107;&#65307;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#26356;&#25442;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33891;&#20107;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall appoint any
designee of Party A as director and/or executive director of Party C, at the request of Party A; without the prior written consent of
Party A, they shall not replace the directors of Party C;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.8 &#24212;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#19981;&#26102;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20010;&#20154;&#20986;&#20855;&#25480;&#26435;&#22996;&#25176;&#20070;&#65292;&#25480;&#26435;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20010;&#20154;&#34892;&#20351;&#19982;&#19993;&#26041;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#32929;&#19996;&#34920;&#20915;&#26435;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall issue such
power of attorney as Party A may request from time to time, to authorize Party A and/or the individual designated by Party A to exercise
Party B&rsquo;s voting rights as a shareholder in Party C.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.9&nbsp;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#38543;&#26102;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#24212;&#21521;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20195;&#34920;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#26102;&#38388;&#26080;&#26465;&#20214;&#22320;&#26681;&#25454;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#31435;&#21363;&#36716;&#35753;&#20854;&#32929;&#26435;&#65292;&#24182;&#25918;&#24323;&#20854;&#23545;&#21478;&#19968;&#29616;&#26377;&#32929;&#19996;&#36827;&#34892;&#20854;&#30456;&#24212;&#32929;&#26435;&#36716;&#35753;&#25152;&#20139;&#26377;&#30340;&#20248;&#20808;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#65288;&#22914;&#26377;&#30340;&#35805;&#65289;&#65307;&#21644;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">At the request of Party A
at any time, Party B shall promptly and unconditionally transfer its equity interests in Party C to Party A&rsquo;s Designee(s) in accordance
with the Equity Interest Purchase Option under this Agreement, and Party B hereby waives its right of first refusal to the respective
share transfer by the other existing shareholder of Party C (if any); and</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2.10&nbsp;&#20005;&#26684;&#36981;&#23432;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21450;&#20057;&#26041;&#12289;&#19993;&#26041;&#19982;&#30002;&#26041;&#20849;&#21516;&#25110;&#20998;&#21035;&#31614;&#35746;&#30340;&#20854;&#20182;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#21508;&#39033;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#20999;&#23454;&#23653;&#34892;&#35813;&#31561;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#21508;&#39033;&#20041;&#21153;&#65292;&#24182;&#19981;&#36827;&#34892;&#20219;&#20309;&#36275;&#20197;&#24433;&#21709;&#35813;&#31561;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#26377;&#25928;&#24615;&#21644;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#24615;&#30340;&#20316;&#20026;/&#19981;&#20316;&#20026;&#12290;&#22914;&#26524;&#20057;&#26041;&#23545;&#20110;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#25110;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21508;&#26041;&#31614;&#32626;&#30340;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#25110;&#23545;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20010;&#20154;&#20986;&#20855;&#30340;&#25480;&#26435;&#22996;&#25176;&#20070;&#20013;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#65292;&#36824;&#30041;&#23384;&#26377;&#20219;&#20309;&#26435;&#21033;&#65292;&#38500;&#38750;&#30002;&#26041;&#20070;&#38754;&#25351;&#31034;&#65292;&#21542;&#21017;&#20057;&#26041;&#20173;&#19981;&#24471;&#34892;&#20351;&#35813;&#26435;&#21033;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B shall strictly abide
by the provisions of this Agreement and other contracts jointly or separately executed by and among Party B, Party C and Party A, perform
the obligations hereunder and thereunder, and refrain from any action/omission that may affect the effectiveness and enforceability thereof.
If Party B retains any additional rights other than those rights provided for under this Agreement, Party B&rsquo;s Equity Pledge Agreement
and the powers of attorney issued to Party A and/or the individual designated by Party A, Party B shall not exercise such rights without
Party A&rsquo;s written direction.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>3. &#38472;&#36848;&#21644;&#20445;&#35777;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in"><B>Representations and Warranties</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#20057;&#26041;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#29305;&#27492;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#31614;&#32626;&#20043;&#26085;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#20849;&#21516;&#21450;&#20998;&#21035;&#38472;&#36848;&#21644;&#20445;&#35777;&#22914;&#19979;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 23.9pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B and Party C hereby
represent and warrant to Party A, jointly and severally, as of the date of this Agreement that:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 22.35pt; text-indent: 0.5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.1&nbsp;&#20854;&#20855;&#26377;&#31614;&#35746;&#21644;&#20132;&#20184;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#20854;&#20026;&#19968;&#26041;&#30340;&#12289;&#26681;&#25454;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20026;&#27599;&#19968;&#27425;&#36716;&#35753;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#32780;&#31614;&#35746;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#32929;&#26435;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;(&#21508;&#31216;&#20026;&ldquo;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&rdquo;)&#65292;&#24182;&#23653;&#34892;&#20854;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#20219;&#20309;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20041;&#21153;&#30340;&#26435;&#21147;&#21644;&#33021;&#21147;&#12290;&#20057;&#26041;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#21516;&#24847;&#22312;&#30002;&#26041;&#34892;&#20351;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#26102;&#65292;&#20182;&#20204;&#23558;&#31614;&#32626;&#19982;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#26465;&#27454;&#19968;&#33268;&#30340;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#12290;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#20854;&#26159;&#19968;&#26041;&#30340;&#21508;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#19968;&#26086;&#31614;&#32626;&#21518;&#65292;&#26500;&#25104;&#25110;&#23558;&#23545;&#20854;&#26500;&#25104;&#21512;&#27861;&#12289;&#26377;&#25928;&#21450;&#20855;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#30340;&#20041;&#21153;&#24182;&#21487;&#25353;&#29031;&#20854;&#26465;&#27454;&#23545;&#20854;&#24378;&#21046;&#25191;&#34892;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">They have the authority to
execute and deliver this Agreement and any share transfer contracts to which they are parties concerning the Optioned Interests to be
transferred thereunder (each, a &ldquo;Transfer Contract&rdquo;), and to perform their obligations under this Agreement and any Transfer
Contracts. Party B and Party C agree to enter into Transfer Contracts consistent with the terms of this Agreement upon Party A&rsquo;s
exercise of the Equity Interest Purchase Option. This Agreement and the Transfer Contracts to which they are parties constitute or will
constitute their legal, valid and binding obligations and shall be enforceable against them in accordance with the provisions thereof;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.2&nbsp;&#26080;&#35770;&#26159;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#31614;&#32626;&#21644;&#20132;&#20184;&#36824;&#26159;&#20854;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20041;&#21153;&#30340;&#23653;&#34892;&#22343;&#19981;&#20250;&#65306;(i)&#23548;&#33268;&#36829;&#21453;&#20219;&#20309;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#65307;(ii)&#19982;&#19993;&#26041;&#31456;&#31243;&#25110;&#20854;&#20182;&#32452;&#32455;&#25991;&#20214;&#30456;&#25269;&#35302;&#65307;(iii)&#23548;&#33268;&#36829;&#21453;&#20854;&#26159;&#19968;&#26041;&#25110;&#23545;&#20854;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#21512;&#21516;&#25110;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#25110;&#26500;&#25104;&#20854;&#26159;&#19968;&#26041;&#25110;&#23545;&#20854;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#21512;&#21516;&#25110;&#25991;&#20214;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#36829;&#32422;&#65307;(iv)&#23548;&#33268;&#36829;&#21453;&#26377;&#20851;&#21521;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#39041;&#21457;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#35768;&#21487;&#25110;&#25209;&#20934;&#30340;&#25480;&#20104;&#21644;(&#25110;)&#32487;&#32493;&#26377;&#25928;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#26465;&#20214;&#65307;&#25110;(v)&#23548;&#33268;&#21521;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#39041;&#21457;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#35768;&#21487;&#25110;&#25209;&#20934;&#20013;&#27490;&#25110;&#34987;&#25764;&#38144;&#25110;&#38468;&#21152;&#26465;&#20214;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">The execution and delivery
of this Agreement or any Transfer Contracts and the obligations under this Agreement or any Transfer Contracts shall not: (i) cause any
violation of any applicable laws of China; (ii) be inconsistent with the articles of association, bylaws or other organizational documents
of Party C; (iii) cause the violation of any contracts or instruments to which they are a party or which are binding on them, or constitute
any breach under any contracts or instruments to which they are a party or which are binding on them; (iv) cause any violation of any
condition for the grant and/or continued effectiveness of any licenses or permits issued to either of them; or (v) cause the suspension
or revocation of or imposition of additional conditions to any licenses or permits issued to either of them;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->9<!-- Field: /Sequence -->&nbsp;</P><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.3 &#20057;&#26041;&#23545;&#20854;&#22312;&#19993;&#26041;&#25317;&#26377;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#25317;&#26377;&#33391;&#22909;&#21644;&#21487;&#20986;&#21806;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#65292;&#38500;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#22806;&#65292;&#20057;&#26041;&#22312;&#19978;&#36848;&#32929;&#26435;&#19978;&#27809;&#26377;&#35774;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party B has a good and merchantable
title to the equity interests in Party C he holds. Except for Party B&rsquo;s Equity Pledge Agreement, Party B has not placed any security interest
on such equity interests;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.4 &#19993;&#26041;&#23545;&#25152;&#26377;&#36164;&#20135;&#25317;&#26377;&#33391;&#22909;&#21644;&#21487;&#20986;&#21806;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#22312;&#19978;&#36848;&#36164;&#20135;&#19978;&#27809;&#26377;&#35774;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party C has a good and merchantable
title to all of its assets, and has not placed any security interest on the aforementioned assets;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.5 &#19993;&#26041;&#27809;&#26377;&#20219;&#20309;&#26410;&#20607;&#36824;&#20538;&#21153;&#65292;&#38500;(i)&#22312;&#20854;&#27491;&#24120;&#30340;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#20538;&#21153;&#65292;&#21450;(ii)&#24050;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#25259;&#38706;&#21450;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#20538;&#21153;&#38500;&#22806;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Party C does not have any
outstanding debts, except for (i) debt incurred in the ordinary course of business; and (ii) debts disclosed to Party A for which Party

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.7 &#30446;&#21069;&#27809;&#26377;&#24748;&#32780;&#26410;&#20915;&#30340;&#25110;&#26500;&#25104;&#23041;&#32961;&#30340;&#19982;&#32929;&#26435;&#12289;&#19993;&#26041;&#36164;&#20135;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#25110;&#19982;&#19993;&#26041;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#35785;&#35772;&#12289;&#20210;&#35009;&#25110;&#34892;&#25919;&#31243;&#24207;&#12290;</P>

litigation, arbitration or administrative proceedings relating to the equity interests in Party C, assets of Party C or Party C.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20110;&#21508;&#26041;&#31614;&#32626;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20043;&#26085;&#29983;&#25928;&#65292;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#22312;&#20057;&#26041;&#25317;&#26377;&#30340;&#20840;&#37096;&#19993;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#26681;&#25454;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#30340;&#32422;&#23450;&#20381;&#27861;&#36716;&#35753;&#33267;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;/&#25110;&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#21517;&#19979;&#21518;&#32456;&#27490;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>5. &#36866;&#29992;&#27861;&#24459;&#19982;&#20105;&#35758;&#35299;&#20915;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in"><B>Governing Law and Resolution
of Disputes</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 10; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->10<!-- Field: /Sequence -->&nbsp;</P><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">5.1 &#36866;&#29992;&#27861;&#24459;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Governing law</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.3pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#35746;&#31435;&#12289;&#25928;&#21147;&#12289;&#35299;&#37322;&#12289;&#23653;&#34892;&#12289;&#20462;&#25913;&#21644;&#32456;&#27490;&#20197;&#21450;&#20105;&#35758;&#35299;&#20915;&#22343;&#36866;&#29992;&#20013;&#22269;&#27491;&#24335;&#20844;&#24067;&#24182;&#21487;&#20844;&#24320;&#24471;&#21040;&#30340;&#27861;&#24459;&#12290;&#23545;&#20013;&#22269;&#27491;&#24335;&#20844;&#24067;&#24182;&#21487;&#20844;&#24320;&#24471;&#21040;&#30340;&#27861;&#24459;&#27809;&#26377;&#35268;&#23450;&#30340;&#20107;&#39033;&#65292;&#23558;&#36866;&#29992;&#22269;&#38469;&#27861;&#24459;&#21407;&#21017;&#21644;&#24815;&#20363;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">The execution, effectiveness,
construction, performance, amendment and termination of this Agreement and the resolution of disputes hereunder shall be governed by the
formally published and publicly available laws of China. Matters not covered by formally published and publicly available laws of China
shall be governed by international legal principles and practices.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.1pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">5.2 &#20105;&#35758;&#30340;&#35299;&#20915;&#26041;&#27861;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Methods of Resolution of
Disputes</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.3pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#22240;&#35299;&#37322;&#21644;&#23653;&#34892;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32780;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20105;&#35758;&#65292;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#39318;&#20808;&#36890;&#36807;&#21451;&#22909;&#21327;&#21830;&#30340;&#26041;&#24335;&#21152;&#20197;&#35299;&#20915;&#12290;&#22914;&#26524;&#22312;&#19968;&#26041;&#21521;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#21457;&#20986;&#35201;&#27714;&#21327;&#21830;&#35299;&#20915;&#30340;&#20070;&#38754;&#36890;&#30693;&#21518;30&#22825;&#20043;&#20869;&#20105;&#35758;&#20173;&#28982;&#24471;&#19981;&#21040;&#35299;&#20915;&#65292;&#21017;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#22343;&#21487;&#23558;&#26377;&#20851;&#20105;&#35758;&#25552;&#20132;&#32473;&#20301;&#20110;&#28145;&#22323;&#30340;&#20013;&#22269;&#22269;&#38469;&#32463;&#27982;&#36152;&#26131;&#20210;&#35009;&#22996;&#21592;&#20250;&#21326;&#21335;&#20998;&#20250;&#65292;&#30001;&#35813;&#20250;&#25353;&#29031;&#20013;&#22269;&#22269;&#38469;&#32463;&#27982;&#36152;&#26131;&#20210;&#35009;&#22996;&#21592;&#20250;&#20210;&#35009;&#35268;&#21017;&#20210;&#35009;&#35299;&#20915;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#24212;&#22312;&#28145;&#22323;&#36827;&#34892;&#65292;&#20351;&#29992;&#20043;&#35821;&#35328;&#20026;&#20013;&#25991;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#35009;&#20915;&#26159;&#32456;&#23616;&#24615;&#30340;&#65292;&#23545;&#21508;&#26041;&#22343;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">In the event of any dispute
with respect to the construction and performance of this Agreement, the Parties shall first resolve the dispute through friendly negotiations.
In the event the Parties fail to reach an agreement on the dispute within 30 days after either Party&rsquo;s request to the other Parties for
resolution of the dispute through negotiations, either Party may submit the relevant dispute to the Southern China Commission of China
International Economic and Trade Arbitration Commission for arbitration, in accordance with its Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall
be conducted in Shenzhen, and the language used in arbitration shall be Chinese. The arbitration award shall be final and binding on all
Parties.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>6. &#31246;&#27454;&#12289;&#36153;&#29992;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in"><B>Taxes and Fees</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#27599;&#19968;&#26041;&#24212;&#25215;&#25285;&#26681;&#25454;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#22240;&#20934;&#22791;&#21644;&#31614;&#32626;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#21508;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#20197;&#21450;&#23436;&#25104;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#21508;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#25311;&#23450;&#30340;&#20132;&#26131;&#32780;&#30001;&#35813;&#26041;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#25110;&#23545;&#20854;&#24449;&#25910;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#21644;&#20840;&#37096;&#30340;&#36716;&#35753;&#21644;&#27880;&#20876;&#30340;&#31246;&#12289;&#33457;&#36153;&#21644;&#36153;&#29992;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Each Party shall pay any
and all transfer and registration tax, expenses and fees incurred thereby or levied thereon in accordance with the laws of China in connection
with the preparation and execution of this Agreement and the Transfer Contracts, as well as the consummation of the transactions contemplated
under this Agreement and the Transfer Contracts.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">7.1&nbsp;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#35201;&#27714;&#25110;&#21457;&#20986;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#36890;&#30693;&#21644;&#20854;&#20182;&#36890;&#20449;&#24212;&#36890;&#36807;&#19987;&#20154;&#36882;&#36865;&#12289;&#25346;&#21495;&#37038;&#23492;&#12289;&#37038;&#36164;&#39044;&#20184;&#25110;&#21830;&#19994;&#24555;&#36882;&#26381;&#21153;&#30340;&#26041;&#24335;&#21457;&#21040;&#35813;&#26041;&#19979;&#21015;&#22320;&#22336;&#12290;&#27599;&#19968;&#36890;&#30693;&#36824;&#24212;&#20877;&#20197;&#30005;&#23376;&#37038;&#20214;&#36865;&#36798;&#12290;&#35813;&#31561;&#36890;&#30693;&#35270;&#20026;&#26377;&#25928;&#36865;&#36798;&#30340;&#26085;&#26399;&#25353;&#22914;&#19979;&#26041;&#24335;&#30830;&#23450;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">All notices and other communications
required or permitted to be given pursuant to this Agreement shall be delivered personally or sent by registered mail, postage prepaid,
by a commercial courier service to the address of such Party set forth below. A confirmation copy of each notice shall also be sent by
email. The dates on which notices shall be deemed to have been effectively given shall be determined as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">7.2&#36890;&#30693;&#22914;&#26524;&#26159;&#20197;&#19987;&#20154;&#36882;&#36865;&#12289;&#24555;&#36882;&#26381;&#21153;&#25110;&#25346;&#21495;&#37038;&#23492;&#12289;&#37038;&#36164;&#39044;&#20184;&#21457;&#20986;&#30340;&#65292;&#21017;&#20197;&#20110;&#35774;&#23450;&#20026;&#36890;&#30693;&#30340;&#22320;&#22336;&#22312;&#31614;&#25910;&#25110;&#25298;&#25910;&#20043;&#26085;&#20026;&#26377;&#25928;&#36865;&#36798;&#26085;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Notices given by personal
delivery, by courier service or by registered mail, postage prepaid, shall be deemed effectively given on the date of acceptance or refusal
at the address specified for notices.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 78pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">7.3 &#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#21464;&#26356;&#25509;&#25910;&#36890;&#30693;&#30340;&#22320;&#22336;&#25110;&#32852;&#31995;&#20154;&#30340;&#65292;&#24212;&#25353;&#26412;&#26465;&#35268;&#23450;&#32473;&#21478;&#19968;&#26041;&#21457;&#20986;&#36890;&#30693;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>8. &#20445;&#23494;&#36131;&#20219;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in"><B>Confidentiality</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#21508;&#26041;&#25215;&#35748;&#21450;&#30830;&#23450;&#26377;&#20851;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#12289;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20869;&#23481;&#65292;&#20197;&#21450;&#24444;&#27492;&#23601;&#20934;&#22791;&#25110;&#23653;&#34892;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32780;&#20132;&#25442;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#21475;&#22836;&#25110;&#20070;&#38754;&#36164;&#26009;&#22343;&#34987;&#35270;&#20026;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#12290;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#24403;&#23545;&#25152;&#26377;&#35813;&#31561;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#20104;&#20197;&#20445;&#23494;&#65292;&#32780;&#22312;&#26410;&#24471;&#21040;&#21478;&#19968;&#26041;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#21069;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#21521;&#20219;&#20309;&#31532;&#19977;&#32773;&#25259;&#38706;&#20219;&#20309;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#65292;&#24799;&#19979;&#21015;&#20449;&#24687;&#38500;&#22806;&#65306;(a)&#20844;&#20247;&#20154;&#22763;&#30693;&#24713;&#25110;&#23558;&#20250;&#30693;&#24713;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20449;&#24687;&#65288;&#24799;&#24182;&#38750;&#30001;&#25509;&#21463;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#20043;&#19968;&#26041;&#25797;&#33258;&#21521;&#20844;&#20247;&#25259;&#38706;&#65289;&#65307;(b)&#26681;&#25454;&#36866;&#29992;&#27861;&#24459;&#27861;&#35268;&#12289;&#32929;&#31080;&#20132;&#26131;&#35268;&#21017;&#12289;&#25110;&#25919;&#24220;&#37096;&#38376;&#25110;&#27861;&#38498;&#30340;&#21629;&#20196;&#32780;&#25152;&#38656;&#25259;&#38706;&#20043;&#20219;&#20309;&#20449;&#24687;&#65307;&#25110;(c)&#30001;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#23601;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25152;&#36848;&#20132;&#26131;&#32780;&#38656;&#21521;&#20854;&#32929;&#19996;&#12289;&#25237;&#36164;&#32773;&#12289;&#27861;&#24459;&#25110;&#36130;&#21153;&#39038;&#38382;&#25259;&#38706;&#20043;&#20449;&#24687;&#65292;&#32780;&#35813;&#32929;&#19996;&#12289;&#27861;&#24459;&#25110;&#36130;&#21153;&#39038;&#38382;&#20134;&#38656;&#36981;&#23432;&#19982;&#26412;&#26465;&#27454;&#30456;&#31867;&#20284;&#20043;&#20445;&#23494;&#36131;&#20219;&#12290;&#22914;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#24037;&#20316;&#20154;&#21592;&#25110;&#32856;&#35831;&#26426;&#26500;&#30340;&#27844;&#23494;&#22343;&#35270;&#20026;&#35813;&#26041;&#30340;&#27844;&#23494;&#65292;&#38656;&#20381;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25215;&#25285;&#36829;&#32422;&#36131;&#20219;&#12290;&#26080;&#35770;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20197;&#20219;&#20309;&#29702;&#30001;&#32456;&#27490;&#65292;&#26412;&#26465;&#27454;&#20173;&#28982;&#29983;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.25pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.05pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">The Parties acknowledge that
the existence and the terms of this Agreement and any oral or written information exchanged between the Parties in connection with the
preparation and performance this Agreement are regarded as confidential information. Each Party shall maintain confidentiality of all
such confidential information, and without obtaining the written consent of the other Party, it shall not disclose any relevant confidential
information to any third parties, except for the information that: (a) is or will be in the public domain (other than through the receiving
Party&rsquo;s unauthorized disclosure); (b) is under the obligation to be disclosed pursuant to the applicable laws or regulations, rules
of any stock exchange, or orders of the court or other government authorities; or (c) is required to be disclosed by any Party to its
shareholders, investors, legal counsels or financial advisors regarding the transaction contemplated hereunder, provided that such shareholders,
investors, legal counsels or financial advisors shall be bound by the confidentiality obligations similar to those set forth in this Section.
Disclosure of any confidential information by the staff members or agencies hired by any Party shall be deemed disclosure of such confidential
information by such Party, which Party shall be held liable for breach of this Agreement. This Section shall survive the termination of
this Agreement for any reason.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.25pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.05pt">&nbsp;</P>

supplements or changes in writing executed after the execution of this Agreement, this Agreement shall constitute the entire agreement
reached by and among the Parties hereto with respect to the subject matter hereof, and shall supercede all prior oral and written consultations,

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.4 &#35821;&#35328;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20197;&#20013;&#25991;&#21644;&#33521;&#25991;&#20070;&#23601;&#65292;&#19968;&#24335;&#19977;&#20221;&#65292;&#30002;&#20057;&#19993;&#19977;&#26041;&#21508;&#25345;&#19968;&#20221;&#65292;&#20855;&#26377;&#21516;&#31561;&#25928;&#21147;&#65307;&#20013;&#33521;&#25991;&#29256;&#26412;&#22914;&#26377;&#20914;&#31361;&#65292;&#24212;&#20197;&#20013;&#25991;&#29256;&#20026;&#20934;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 56.7pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">This Agreement is written

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.5 &#21487;&#20998;&#21106;&#24615;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Severability</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.3pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#22914;&#26524;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#26377;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26465;&#25110;&#22810;&#26465;&#35268;&#23450;&#26681;&#25454;&#20219;&#20309;&#27861;&#24459;&#25110;&#27861;&#35268;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#26041;&#38754;&#34987;&#35009;&#23450;&#20026;&#26080;&#25928;&#12289;&#19981;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#19981;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#65292;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20854;&#20313;&#35268;&#23450;&#30340;&#26377;&#25928;&#24615;&#12289;&#21512;&#27861;&#24615;&#25110;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#24615;&#19981;&#24212;&#22240;&#27492;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#26041;&#38754;&#21463;&#21040;&#24433;&#21709;&#25110;&#25439;&#23475;&#12290;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#36890;&#36807;&#35802;&#24847;&#30923;&#21830;&#65292;&#20105;&#21462;&#20197;&#27861;&#24459;&#35768;&#21487;&#20197;&#21450;&#21508;&#26041;&#26399;&#26395;&#30340;&#26368;&#22823;&#38480;&#24230;&#20869;&#26377;&#25928;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#21462;&#20195;&#37027;&#20123;&#26080;&#25928;&#12289;&#19981;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#19981;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#32780;&#35813;&#31561;&#26377;&#25928;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#25152;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#32463;&#27982;&#25928;&#26524;&#24212;&#23613;&#21487;&#33021;&#19982;&#37027;&#20123;&#26080;&#25928;&#12289;&#19981;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#19981;&#33021;&#24378;&#21046;&#25191;&#34892;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#25152;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#32463;&#27982;&#25928;&#26524;&#30456;&#20284;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 56.7pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">In the event that one or
several of the provisions of this Agreement are found to be invalid, illegal or unenforceable in any aspect in accordance with any laws
or regulations, the validity, legality or enforceability of the remaining provisions of this Agreement shall not be affected or compromised
in any respect. The Parties shall strive in good faith to replace such invalid, illegal or unenforceable provisions with effective provisions
that accomplish to the greatest extent permitted by law and the intentions of the Parties, and the economic effect of such effective provisions
shall be as close as possible to the economic effect of those invalid, illegal or unenforceable provisions.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.6 &#32487;&#20219;&#32773;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Successors</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.3pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#23545;&#21508;&#26041;&#21508;&#33258;&#30340;&#32487;&#20219;&#32773;&#21644;&#21508;&#26041;&#25152;&#20801;&#35768;&#30340;&#21463;&#35753;&#26041;&#24212;&#20855;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#24182;&#23545;&#20854;&#26377;&#21033;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 56.7pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">This Agreement shall be binding
on and shall inure to the interest of the respective successors of the Parties and the permitted assigns of such Parties.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 56.7pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.7 &#24323;&#26435;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Waivers</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.3pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#21487;&#20197;&#23545;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#26465;&#27454;&#21644;&#26465;&#20214;&#20316;&#20986;&#24323;&#26435;&#65292;&#20294;&#24517;&#39035;&#32463;&#20070;&#38754;&#20316;&#20986;&#24182;&#32463;&#21508;&#26041;&#31614;&#23383;&#12290;&#19968;&#26041;&#22312;&#26576;&#31181;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;&#23601;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#30340;&#36829;&#32422;&#25152;&#20316;&#30340;&#24323;&#26435;&#19981;&#24212;&#34987;&#35270;&#20026;&#35813;&#26041;&#22312;&#20854;&#20182;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;&#23601;&#31867;&#20284;&#30340;&#36829;&#32422;&#24050;&#32463;&#23545;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#20316;&#20986;&#24323;&#26435;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 56.7pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Any Party may waive the terms
and conditions of this Agreement, provided that such a waiver must be provided in writing and shall require the signatures of the Parties.
No waiver by any Party in certain circumstances with respect to a breach by other Parties shall operate as a waiver by such a Party with
respect to any similar breach in other circumstances.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 56.7pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.8 &#32487;&#32493;&#26377;&#25928;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Survival</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.8.1 &#21512;&#21516;&#26399;&#28385;&#25110;&#25552;&#21069;&#32456;&#27490;&#21069;&#22240;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32780;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#25110;&#21040;&#26399;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20041;&#21153;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#26399;&#28385;&#25110;&#25552;&#21069;&#32456;&#27490;&#21518;&#32487;&#32493;&#26377;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">Any obligations that occur
or that are due as a result of this Agreement upon the expiration or early termination of this Agreement shall survive the expiration
or early termination thereof.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 92.15pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.8.2 &#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#31532;5&#12289;7&#12289;8&#26465;&#21644;&#26412;&#31532;10.8&#26465;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32456;&#27490;&#21518;&#32487;&#32493;&#26377;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">The provisions of Sections
5, 7, 8 and this Section 10.8 shall survive the termination of this Agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 92.15pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">10.9 &#34917;&#20607;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 50.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 50.45pt"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->15<!-- Field: /Sequence -->&nbsp;</P><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>
